park-Boat-Hull,note,"Residents: Parking in the main parking lot at the ferry, as well as in other posted areas near the ferry, is restricted to Hull residents with a municipal parking sticker issued by the Town of Hull. | Non-residents: Free non-restricted parking is available in the parking lot at the end of Helen Street, as well as in the high school parking lot (This is only allowed when school is NOT in session). There is also non-restricted parking located at the Stony Beach parking lot (across from the Hull Sewer Plant located at 1111 Nantasket Ave.). This lot is located along the MBTA bus route. To park here you would need to allow extra time to take the bus from the lot to the ferry. All parking restrictions in the ferry parking lots and high school lots are strictly enforced by the Hull Police Department year round. The Town of Hull is responsible for snow removal and maintenance."
